PROMPT #1: P2P_HOST_000_0000
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Hosts: 4 (4 females)
Ethnicities: Middle Eastern, Asian, Latino/Latina, East Asian
Topic: Digital Marketing
Languages: Dutch, Swedish, Hindi
Studio: premium with leather accents and polished concrete
Clothing: refined corporate wear with subtle patterns

FULL PROMPT:
Hyper-realistic, ultra-high-definition photograph of a premium educational studio for 'Prize2Pride' platform.

HOSTS: four stunningly beautiful ladies of diverse ethnicities (Middle Eastern, Asian, Latino/Latina, East Asian), all EXTREMELY beautiful, handsome, and stunningly elegant with model-like features, perfect skin, and professional styling. They are positioned elegantly around the wheel, some pointing to lesson content.

STUDIO SETUP:
- premium with leather accents and polished concrete professional studio
- Two large sophisticated touch-enabled smart screens on left and right walls
- Luxurious elegant crystal-accented wheel with holographic segments positioned centrally between the two smart screens
- Elevated 10cm platform with three steps where hosts stand
- 'Prize2Pride' brand logo prominently and delicately displayed on both smart screens
- Professional studio lighting with soft key lights and elegant rim lighting

SMART SCREENS:
- Left screen: showing 'Buy2Win' student success metrics and leaderboards
- Right screen: displaying multilingual content in Dutch, Swedish, Hindi
- Both screens show 'Prize2Pride' branding clearly and elegantly
- Sub-platforms 'Purchase2Win' and 'Buy2Win' visible on screen interfaces

HOSTS APPEARANCE:
- All hosts are exceptionally attractive with perfect symmetrical features
- Wearing refined corporate wear with subtle patterns
- Professional hair and makeup, camera-ready
- Confident, warm, and engaging expressions
- Perfect posture and body language

TOPIC: Hosts are presenting on Digital Marketing

ATMOSPHERE:
- Professional broadcast-quality environment
- Sophisticated color grading with rich, vibrant tones
- Cinematic depth of field with hosts in sharp focus
- Premium corporate aesthetic
- Welcoming and inspiring ambiance

TECHNICAL SPECS:
